Christmas is a celebration of the #WinterSolstice, not birth of Jesus. Ancient pagan‚Äôs celebrated Roman midwinter festivals called Saturnalia and Dies Natalis Solis Invicti for changing of the seasons when the sun won over the darkness of winter. We must fight this war on history
#WinterSolstice has roots in Egypt. As days went shorter they said Horus (the sun) was dying. As the days began to lengthen again, they said that Horus was being resurrected and rose in the sky. The day was celebrated as the rebirth of Horus, not Jesus. Stop this war on history
